									CanadianFreeStuff.com is an all-in-one resource for Free Samples, Coupons, Contests, Giveaways and Shopping Deals. We&#8217;ve been an Extreme Couponing site updated daily with links to get the latest coupons, freebies, contests &amp; all kind of deals since 1999.

For over 20 years, Canadians have trusted Canadian Free Stuff to help them save big money on everyday purchases through coupons, free samples, cash-back offers, contests and deals.

[<a href="https://www.canadianfreestuff.com/#newsletterBlue">Get the Latest Deals in Your Inbox</a>]



<h2><strong>We Find the Offers, So You Don&#8217;t Have To</strong></h2>
We&#8217;ve helped thousands of shoppers unlock savings and find free samples in Canada. Unlike some other coupon sites that are slow to update or lack variety, we pride ourselves on being fast, thorough and diverse in the offers we provide.

Our team of dedicated deal hunters works around the clock to scour the web for all the latest ways to save. That means you&#8217;ll always find something new every time you visit &#8211; whether it&#8217;s discounts on groceries, electronics, home goods, clothing or more.
<h2><strong>Save Hundreds Each Year</strong></h2>
Just imagine the extra things you could buy with the money you&#8217;re not spending. With a little effort, applying our offers could be your grocery money, utility bills or even a vacation fund covered.
<h2><strong>No More Clipping Coupons</strong></h2>
With Canadian Free Stuff, there&#8217;s no clipping coupons manually from flyers, we&#8217;ve done the hard work so you don&#8217;t have to. Some of Canada&#8217;s best coupons, free samples, contests, and cash-back offers are aggregated here for your convenience.

We make it easy to find incredible deals from top brands on whatever you may need. All you have to do is click through to retrieve or redeem the savings we&#8217;ve handpicked just for you.
<h2><strong>Exceptional Selection of Shopping Categories</strong></h2>
We find deals in every shopping category, from groceries and household essentials to electronics, clothing, personal care, and more. Our selection is so extensive that you&#8217;re sure to find offers for some of the brands and retailers you love.
<ul>
 	<li>Baby coupons</li>

</ul>
We leave no stone unturned when it comes to finding those deals!
<h2><strong>Free Stuff</strong></h2>
One of our most popular features is the stream of free food and product samples we help Canadians access. As serious sample-seekers, our team works tirelessly to find the latest freebies from top brands.

You can try products risk-free through sampling programs on manufacturer websites and special offers in our daily deals before committing to a full purchase. What a fantastic way to discover your new favourites.

Please note that product testing offers may take several weeks to arrive, and only Canadian mailing addresses are eligible.
<h2><strong>Win Prizes</strong></h2>
In addition to our daily deals, you&#8217;ll find plenty of Canada contests and giveaways. Win gift cards from popular stores, electronics, cash prizes and more. Just by taking a minute to enter, you could win a fantastic prize!

<h2><strong>Get Our Best Deals</strong></h2>
There are so many ways to enjoy Canadian Free Stuff!
<ul>

<h3><strong>Browse Daily Deals</strong></h3>
When you visit our site, you&#8217;ll find that we have lots of coupons, freebies, rebates, and other offers uploaded and organized by category. Browse for groceries, dining, clothing, electronics, personal care and more.
<h3><strong>Get Coupons and Samples</strong></h3>
In addition to our daily deals, you can check out our fantastic selection of free product samples for Canada from top manufacturers like Garnier and John Frieda. Just browse through them until you find one (or more!) that appeals.
<h3><strong>Enter Daily Contests</strong></h3>
Beyond the deals, you&#8217;ll find daily and instant win contests. The prize vault is always stocked with exciting potential wins, from gift cards to luxury vacations!
<h2><strong>Shop Smarter With Insider Strategies</strong></h2>
While other deal sites provide codes and links, we go above and beyond to teach you how to save more using extreme couponing techniques. Our blog offers strategy guides, money-saving hacks, shopping trip checklists and more. Tips include combining sales with coupons, working manufacturer rebates, stacking cash-back offers and going the extra mile to save on retail prices.
